rp_timer_irq_callback timer callback\n *\n * @param obj pointer to the radioplanner object itself\n */\nstatic void rp_timer_irq_callback( void* obj );\n\n/**\n * @brief rp_hook_callback call the callback associated to the id\n *\n * @param rp pointer to the radioplanner object itself\n * @param id target hook id\n */\nstatic void rp_hook_callback( radio_planner_t* rp, uint8_t id );\n\n/**\n * @brief rp_task_print debug print function for rp\n *\n * @param rp pointer to the radioplanner object itself\n * @param task target task to print\n */\nstatic void rp_task_print( const radio_planner_t* rp, const rp_task_t* task );\n\n/**\n * @brief print_hook_ids print the hook ids human readable\n */\nstatic void print_hook_ids( void );\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PUBLIC FUNCTIONS DEFINITION ---------------------------------------------\n */\n\nvoid rp_init( radio_planner_t* rp, const ralf_t* radio )\n{\n    memset( rp, 0, sizeof( radio_planner_t ) );\n    rp->radio = radio;\n\n    for( int32_t i = 0; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n    {\n        rp->tasks[i].hook_id                      = i;\n        rp->tasks[i].type                         = RP_TASK_TYPE_NONE;\n        rp->tasks[i].launch_task_callbacks        = NULL;\n        rp->tasks[i].state                        = RP_TASK_STATE_FINISHED;\n        rp->tasks[i].schedule_task_low_priority   = false;\n        rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[i] = rp->radio;\n        rp->hooks[i]                              = NULL;\n        rp->tasks[i].launch_task_callbacks        = NULL;\n        rp->hook_callbacks[i]                     = NULL;\n        rp->status[i]                             = RP_STATUS_TASK_INIT;\n    }\n    rp->priority_task.type  = RP_TASK_TYPE_NONE;\n    rp->priority_task.state = RP_TASK_STATE_FINISHED;\n    rp->radio_is_free       = true;\n    rp_stats_init( &rp->stats );\n    rp->next_state_status = RP_STATUS_NO_MORE_TASK_SCHEDULE;\n    rp->margin_delay      = RP_MARGIN_DELAY;\n    rp->disable_failsafe  = 0;\n    print_hook_ids( );\n}\nrp_hook_status_t rp_attach_new_radio( radio_planner_t* rp, const ralf_t* radio, const uint8_t hook_id )\n{\n    if( hook_id >= RP_NB_HOOKS )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n    if( radio ==\n        rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[hook_id] )  // radio shall not be the same radio as the initial one\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n    rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[hook_id] = radio;\n    return RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n}\nrp_hook_status_t rp_hook_init( radio_planner_t* rp, const uint8_t id, void ( *callback )( void* context ), void* hook )\n{\n    if( id >= RP_NB_HOOKS )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n    if( ( rp->hook_callbacks[id] != NULL ) || ( callback == NULL ) )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n    rp->status[id]         = RP_STATUS_TASK_INIT;\n    rp->hook_callbacks[id] = callback;\n    rp->hooks[id]          = hook;\n\n    return RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n}\n\nrp_hook_status_t rp_release_hook( radio_planner_t* rp, uint8_t id )\n{\n    if( id >= RP_NB_HOOKS )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n\n    rp->hook_callbacks[id]                   = NULL;\n    rp->tasks[id].schedule_task_low_priority = false;\n    return RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n}\n\nrp_hook_status_t rp_hook_get_id( const radio_planner_t* rp, const void* hook, uint8_t* id )\n{\n    for( int32_t i = 0; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n    {\n        if( hook == rp->hooks[i] )\n        {\n            *id = i;\n            return RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n        }\n    }\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n    return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n}\n\nrp_hook_status_t rp_task_enqueue( radio_planner_t* rp, const rp_task_t* task, uint8_t* payload,\n                                  uint16_t payload_buffer_size, const rp_radio_params_t* radio_params )\n{\n    uint8_t hook_id = task->hook_id;\n    if( hook_id >= RP_NB_HOOKS )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n    if( ( task->launch_task_callbacks == NULL ) || ( rp->hook_callbacks[hook_id] == NULL ) )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n    if( ( task->state ) > RP_TASK_STATE_ASAP )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( \" task invalid\\n\" );\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n    uint32_t now = smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( );\n\n    if( ( task->state == RP_TASK_STATE_SCHEDULE ) && ( ( ( int32_t ) ( task->start_time_ms - now ) <= 0 ) ) )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF(\n            \" RP: Task #%u enqueue impossible. Task is in past start_time_ms:%d - now:%d = %d\\n\", hook_id,\n            task->start_time_ms, now, task->start_time_ms - now );\n        return RP_TASK_STATUS_SCHEDULE_TASK_IN_PAST;\n    }\n\n    if( ( ( task->start_time_ms - now ) > 36000000 ) &&\n        ( task->start_time_ms > now ) )  // this task is too far in the future, improve robustness to wrapping issue\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF(\n            \" RP: Task enqueue impossible. Task is too far in future start_time_ms:%d - now:%d = %d\\n\",\n            task->start_time_ms, now, task->start_time_ms - now );\n        return RP_TASK_STATUS_TASK_TOO_FAR_IN_FUTURE;\n    }\n\n    if( rp->tasks[hook_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: Task enqueue impossible. Task is already running\\n\" );\n        return RP_TASK_STATUS_ALREADY_RUNNING;\n    }\n    if( rp->tasks[hook_id].state != RP_TASK_STATE_FINISHED )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: WARNING Task is already running\\n\" );\n    }\n    rp->status[hook_id]              = RP_STATUS_TASK_INIT;\n    rp->tasks[hook_id]               = *task;\n    rp->radio_params[hook_id]        = *radio_params;\n    rp->payload[hook_id]             = payload;\n    rp->payload_buffer_size[hook_id] = payload_buffer_size;\n    if( rp->tasks[hook_id].schedule_task_low_priority == true )\n    {\n        rp->tasks[hook_id].priority = ( RP_TASK_STATE_ASAP * RP_NB_HOOKS ) + hook_id;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        rp->tasks[hook_id].priority = ( rp->tasks[hook_id].state * RP_NB_HOOKS ) + hook_id;\n    }\n    rp->tasks[hook_id].start_time_init_ms = rp->tasks[hook_id].start_time_ms;\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP: Task #%u enqueue with #%u priority\\n\", hook_id, rp->tasks[hook_id].priority );\n    rp_task_compute_ranking( rp );\n    if( rp->radio_irq_flag == false )\n    {\n        rp_task_arbiter( rp, __func__ );\n    }\n    return RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n}\n\nrp_hook_status_t rp_task_abort( radio_planner_t* rp, const uint8_t hook_id )\n{\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP: rp_task_abort #%d\\n\", hook_id );\n    if( hook_id >= RP_NB_HOOKS )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n\n    if( rp->tasks[hook_id].state > RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED )\n    {\n        return RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n    }\n\n    if( rp->tasks[hook_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING )\n    {\n#if defined( ADD_LBM_GEOLOCATION )\n        if( ( hook_id == RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_GNSS ) ||\n            ( hook_id == RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_GNSS_ALMANAC ) || ( hook_id == RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_WIFI ) )\n        {\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n                lr11xx_system_abort_blocking_cmd( rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[hook_id]->ral.context ) ==\n                LR11XX_STATUS_OK );\n        }\n#endif\n        if( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_LOCK_RADIO_ACCESS )\n        {\n            rp->tasks[hook_id].type = RP_TASK_TYPE_UNLOCK_RADIO_ACCESS;\n        }\n        rp->radio_irq_flag                      = true;  // Fake soft IRQ to call user callback\n        rp->irq_timestamp_ms[rp->radio_task_id] = smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( );\n        smtc_modem_hal_user_lbm_irq( );\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        rp->tasks[hook_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED;\n\n        if( rp->radio_irq_flag == false )\n        {\n            rp_task_arbiter( rp, __func__ );\n        }\n    }\n    return RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n}\n\nvoid rp_get_status( const radio_planner_t* rp, const uint8_t id, uint32_t* irq_timestamp_ms, rp_status_t* status )\n{\n    if( id >= RP_NB_HOOKS )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return;\n    }\n    *irq_timestamp_ms = rp->irq_timestamp_ms[id];\n    *status           = rp->status[id];\n}\n\nvoid rp_get_and_clear_raw_radio_irq( radio_planner_t* rp, const uint8_t id, ral_irq_t* raw_radio_irq )\n{\n    if( id >= RP_NB_HOOKS )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return;\n    }\n    *raw_radio_irq        = rp->raw_radio_irq[id];\n    rp->raw_radio_irq[id] = 0;\n}\n\nrp_stats_t rp_get_stats( const radio_planner_t* rp )\n{\n    return rp->stats;\n}\n\nvoid rp_callback( radio_planner_t* rp )\n{\n    if( ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) &&\n        ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type != RP_TASK_TYPE_LOCK_RADIO_ACCESS ) &&\n        ( rp->disable_failsafe != RP_DISABLE_FAILSAFE_KEY ) &&\n        ( ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].start_time_ms + 128000 - smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( ) ) < 0 ) )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( \"RP_FAILSAFE - #%d\\n\", rp->radio_task_id );\n    }\n    if( ( rp->radio_irq_flag == false ) && ( rp->timer_irq_flag == false ) )\n    {\n        return;\n    }\n    if( ( rp->radio_irq_flag == false ) && ( rp->timer_irq_flag == true ) )\n    {\n        rp->timer_irq_flag = false;\n        rp_timer_irq( rp );\n        return;\n    }\n\n    if( rp->radio_irq_flag == true )\n    {\n        rp->radio_irq_flag = false;\n        if( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state < RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED )\n        {\n            if( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_LOCK_RADIO_ACCESS )\n            {\n                rp->status[rp->radio_task_id] = RP_STATUS_RADIO_LOCKED;\n                // update statistic to support direct radio driver access\n                rp_consumption_statistics_updated( rp, rp->radio_task_id, rp->irq_timestamp_ms[rp->radio_task_id] );\n                rp->radio = TARGET_RADIO;\n                rp_hook_callback( rp, rp->radio_task_id );\n                return;\n            }\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: INFO - Radio IRQ received for hook #%u\\n\", rp->radio_task_id );\n\n            rp_irq_get_status( rp, rp->radio_task_id );\n\n            if( rp->status[rp->radio_task_id] == RP_STATUS_LR_FHSS_HOP )\n            {\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // Compute statistics after LR-FHSS hopping interrupts to have the correct TOA and not only by hop\n            rp_consumption_statistics_updated( rp, rp->radio_task_id, rp->irq_timestamp_ms[rp->radio_task_id] );\n\n            // Tx can be performed only if no activity detected on channel\n            if( ( rp->status[rp->radio_task_id] == RP_STATUS_CAD_NEGATIVE ) &&\n                ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_CAD_TO_TX ) )\n            {\n                rp->radio = TARGET_RADIO;\n                rp_hook_callback( rp, rp->radio_task_id );\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // Rx can be performed if activity detected on channel\n            if( ( rp->status[rp->radio_task_id] == RP_STATUS_CAD_POSITIVE ) &&\n                ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_CAD_TO_RX ) )\n            {\n                rp->radio = TARGET_RADIO;\n                rp_hook_callback( rp, rp->radio_task_id );\n                return;\n            }\n\n            if( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE_SCAN )\n            {\n                if( ( rp->status[rp->radio_task_id] == RP_STATUS_RX_PACKET ) ||\n                    ( rp->status[rp->radio_task_id] == RP_STATUS_RX_CRC_ERROR ) )\n                {\n                    rp->radio = TARGET_RADIO;\n                    rp_hook_callback( rp, rp->radio_task_id );\n                    return;\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Have to call rp_task_free before rp_hook_callback because the callback can enqueued a task and so call\n            // the arbiter\n            rp->radio_is_free = false;  // this is a kind of critical section\n            rp_task_free( rp, &rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id] );\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE( ral_set_sleep( TARGET_RAL, true ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n            rp->radio = TARGET_RADIO;\n\n            rp_hook_callback( rp, rp->radio_task_id );\n\n            rp_task_call_aborted( rp );\n            rp->radio_is_free = true;  // end of critical section\n            rp_task_arbiter( rp, __func__ );\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            // A radio irq happened and no rp task is on going, put radio to sleep\n            // even in case multiple radio put only main radio in sleep\n            for( int i = 0; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n            {\n                SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n                    ral_set_sleep( &( rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[i]->ral ), true ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n            }\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \" radio planner it but no more task activated\\n\" );\n        }\n\n        smtc_modem_hal_set_ant_switch( false );\n        // Shut Down the TCXO\n        smtc_modem_hal_stop_radio_tcxo( );\n    }\n}\n\nbool rp_get_irq_flag( void* obj )\n{\n    radio_planner_t* rp = ( ( radio_planner_t* ) obj );\n    if( ( rp->timer_irq_flag == true ) || ( rp->radio_irq_flag == true ) )\n    {\n        return true;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        return false;\n    }\n}\nvoid rp_disable_failsafe( radio_planner_t* rp, bool disable )\n{\n    if( disable == true )\n    {\n        rp->disable_failsafe = RP_DISABLE_FAILSAFE_KEY;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        rp->disable_failsafe = 0;\n    }\n}\n/**\n * @brief Get the status of the radio\n *\n * @return true if the radio isn't used by any task, false otherwise\n */\nbool rp_radio_is_free( radio_planner_t* rp )\n{\n    if( ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) || ( rp->radio_is_free == false ) )\n    {\n        return false;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        return true;\n    }\n}\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PRIVATE FUNCTIONS DEFINITION --------------------------------------------\n */\n\nstatic void rp_task_free( const radio_planner_t* rp, rp_task_t* task )\n{\n    task->hook_id            = RP_NB_HOOKS;\n    task->start_time_ms      = 0;\n    task->start_time_init_ms = 0;\n    task->duration_time_ms   = 0;\n    //   task->type               = RP_TASK_TYPE_NONE; doesn't clear for suspend feature\n    task->state                      = RP_TASK_STATE_FINISHED;\n    task->schedule_task_low_priority = false;\n}\n\nstatic void rp_task_update_time( radio_planner_t* rp, uint32_t now )\n{\n    uint32_t fairness_tmp = 0;\n\n    if( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING )\n    {\n        fairness_tmp = RP_MCU_FAIRNESS_DELAY_MS;\n    }\n\n    for( int32_t i = 0; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n    {\n        if( rp->tasks[i].state == RP_TASK_STATE_ASAP )\n        {\n            if( ( int32_t ) ( now - rp->tasks[i].start_time_ms ) > 0 )\n            {\n                rp->tasks[i].start_time_ms = now + fairness_tmp;\n            }\n\n            // An asap task is automatically switch in schedule task after RP_TASK_ASAP_TO_SCHEDULE_TRIG_TIME ms\n            if( ( int32_t ) ( now - rp->tasks[i].start_time_init_ms ) > RP_TASK_ASAP_TO_SCHEDULE_TRIG_TIME )\n            {\n                rp->tasks[i].state = RP_TASK_STATE_SCHEDULE;\n                // Schedule the task at (now + RP_TASK_RE_SCHEDULE_OFFSET_TIME) seconds\n                rp->tasks[i].start_time_ms = now + RP_TASK_RE_SCHEDULE_OFFSET_TIME;\n                rp->tasks[i].priority      = ( rp->tasks[i].state * RP_NB_HOOKS ) + i;\n                SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_WARNING(\n                    \"RP: SWITCH TASK #%d FROM ASAP TO SCHEDULED (start_time_init_ms:%u, now:%u, diff:%d)\\n\", i,\n                    rp->tasks[i].start_time_init_ms, now, ( int32_t ) ( now - rp->tasks[i].start_time_init_ms ) );\n                rp_task_compute_ranking( rp );\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    if( ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) &&\n        ( ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_LORA ) ||\n          ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_FSK ) ||\n          ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_FLRC ) ||\n          ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE ) ||\n          ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE_SCAN ) ) )\n    {\n        rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].duration_time_ms =\n            now + rp->margin_delay + 2 - rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].start_time_ms;\n        if( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].schedule_task_low_priority == true )\n        {\n            rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].schedule_task_low_priority = false;\n            rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].priority = ( RP_TASK_STATE_SCHEDULE * RP_NB_HOOKS ) + rp->radio_task_id;\n            rp_task_compute_ranking( rp );\n        }\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: Extended duration of radio task #%u time to %u ms\\n\", rp->radio_task_id,\n                                        now );\n    }\n}\n\nstatic void rp_task_arbiter( radio_planner_t* rp, const char* caller_func_name )\n{\n    uint32_t now = smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( );\n    // Update time for ASAP task to now. But, also extended duration in case of running task is a RX task\n    rp_task_update_time( rp, now );\n\n    // Select the high priority task\n    if( rp_task_select_next( rp, now ) == RP_SOMETHING_TO_DO )\n    {  // Next task exists\n        int32_t delay = ( int32_t ) ( rp->priority_task.start_time_ms - now );\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF(\n            \" RP: Arbiter has been called by %s and priority-task #%d, timer hook #%d, delay %d, now %d, start_time_ms \"\n            \"%u\\n\",\n            caller_func_name, rp->priority_task.hook_id, rp->timer_hook_id, delay, now,\n            rp->priority_task.start_time_ms );\n\n        // Case where the high priority task is in the past, error case\n        if( delay < 0 )\n        {  // The high priority task is in the past, error case\n            if( rp->priority_task.state != RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING )\n            {\n                rp->stats.rp_error++;\n                SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_ERROR( \" RP: ERROR - delay #%d - hook #%d\\n\", delay, rp->priority_task.hook_id );\n\n                rp->tasks[rp->priority_task.hook_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED;\n            }\n        }\n        // Case where the high priority task is in the future\n        else if( ( uint32_t ) delay > rp->margin_delay )\n        {  // The high priority task is in the future\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: High priority task is in the future\\n\" );\n        }\n        // Case where the high priority task is now\n        else\n        {\n            if( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING )\n            {  // Radio is already running\n                if( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].hook_id != rp->priority_task.hook_id )\n                {  // priority task not equal to radio task => abort radio task if the priority task is SCHEDULED\n                    rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED;\n                    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP: Abort running #%u for priority #%u\\n\", rp->radio_task_id,\n                                                 rp->priority_task.hook_id );\n#if defined( ADD_LBM_GEOLOCATION )\n                    if( ( rp->radio_task_id == RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_GNSS ) ||\n                        ( rp->radio_task_id == RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_GNSS_ALMANAC ) ||\n                        ( rp->radio_task_id == RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_WIFI ) )\n                    {\n                        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n                            lr11xx_system_abort_blocking_cmd(\n                                rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[rp->radio_task_id]->ral.context ) ==\n                            LR11XX_STATUS_OK );\n                    }\n#endif\n                    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE( ral_set_standby( TARGET_RAL, RAL_STANDBY_CFG_RC ) ==\n                                                     RAL_STATUS_OK );\n                    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE( ral_clear_irq_status( TARGET_RAL, RAL_IRQ_ALL ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n\n                    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE( ral_set_sleep( TARGET_RAL, true ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n\n                    rp->radio_irq_flag = false;\n\n                    smtc_modem_hal_set_ant_switch( false );\n                    // Shut Down the TCXO\n                    smtc_modem_hal_stop_radio_tcxo( );\n\n                    rp_consumption_statistics_updated( rp, rp->radio_task_id, smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( ) );\n                    rp->radio_task_id = rp->priority_task.hook_id;\n                    if( smtc_modem_external_stack_currently_use_radio( ) == true )\n                    {\n                        rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED;\n                    }\n                    else\n                    {\n                        rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING;\n                        rp_task_launch_current( rp );\n                    }\n                }  // else case already managed during enqueue task\n            }\n            else\n            {  // Radio is sleeping start priority task on radio\n                rp->radio_task_id = rp->priority_task.hook_id;\n                if( smtc_modem_external_stack_currently_use_radio( ) == true )\n                {\n                    rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED;\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING;\n                    rp_task_launch_current( rp );\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        // Timer has expired on a not priority task => Have to abort this task\n        int32_t tmp = ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[rp->timer_hook_id].start_time_ms - now );\n\n        if( tmp > 0 )\n        {\n            if( ( ( uint32_t ) tmp < rp->margin_delay ) && ( rp->next_state_status == RP_STATUS_HAVE_TO_SET_TIMER ) &&\n                ( rp->timer_hook_id != rp->priority_task.hook_id ) &&\n                ( rp->tasks[rp->timer_hook_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_SCHEDULE ) )\n            {\n                SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_WARNING( \" RP: Aborted task with hook #%u - not a priority task\\n\",\n                                              rp->timer_hook_id );\n                rp->tasks[rp->timer_hook_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED;\n            }\n        }\n        // Execute the garbage collection if the radio isn't running\n        if( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state != RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING )\n        {\n            rp_task_call_aborted( rp );\n        }\n\n        // Set the Timer to the next Task\n        rp->next_state_status =\n            rp_task_get_next( rp, &rp->timer_value, &rp->timer_hook_id, smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( ) );\n\n        if( rp->next_state_status == RP_STATUS_HAVE_TO_SET_TIMER )\n        {\n            if( rp->timer_value > rp->margin_delay )\n            {\n                rp_set_alarm( rp, rp->timer_value - rp->margin_delay );\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                rp->timer_irq_flag = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    else\n    {  // No more tasks in the radio planner\n        rp_task_call_aborted( rp );\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: No more active tasks\\n\" );\n    }\n}\n\nstatic void rp_irq_get_status( radio_planner_t* rp, const uint8_t hook_id )\n{\n    ral_irq_t radio_irq = 0;\n    if( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_UNLOCK_RADIO_ACCESS )\n    {\n        rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RADIO_UNLOCKED;\n        return;\n    }\n    if( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_LBT )\n    {\n        return;\n    }\n    if( ral_get_and_clear_irq_status( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, &radio_irq ) != RAL_STATUS_OK )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n    }\n\n    if( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE_SCAN )\n    {\n        if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RX_TIMEOUT ) == RAL_IRQ_RX_TIMEOUT )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RX_TIMEOUT;\n        }\n        else if( ( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RX_HDR_ERROR ) == RAL_IRQ_RX_HDR_ERROR ) ||\n                 ( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RX_CRC_ERROR ) == RAL_IRQ_RX_CRC_ERROR ) )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RX_CRC_ERROR;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RX_DONE ) == RAL_IRQ_RX_DONE )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RX_PACKET;\n\n            if( rp_get_pkt_payload( rp, &rp->tasks[hook_id] ) == RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR )\n            {\n                SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n                return;\n            }\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: ERROR SCAN - IRQ source 0x%04X unknown\\n\", radio_irq );\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_TASK_ABORTED;\n        }\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        // Do not modify the order of the next if / else if process\n        rp->raw_radio_irq[hook_id] = radio_irq;\n        if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RTTOF_REQ_DISCARDED ) == RAL_IRQ_RTTOF_REQ_DISCARDED )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RTTOF_REQ_DISCARDED;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RTTOF_RESP_DONE ) == RAL_IRQ_RTTOF_RESP_DONE )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RTTOF_RESP_DONE;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RTTOF_EXCH_VALID ) == RAL_IRQ_RTTOF_EXCH_VALID )\n        {\n            int32_t raw_distance  = 0;\n            int32_t results_meter = 0;\n            int8_t  rssi_result   = 0;\n\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n                ral_rttof_get_raw_result( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, rp->radio_params[hook_id].rttof.bw_ranging,\n                                          &raw_distance, &results_meter, &rssi_result ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n\n            rp->radio_params[hook_id].rttof.ranging_result->distance_m   = results_meter;\n            rp->radio_params[hook_id].rttof.ranging_result->rssi         = rssi_result;\n            rp->radio_params[hook_id].rttof.ranging_result->raw_distance = raw_distance;\n\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RTTOF_EXCH_VALID;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RTTOF_TIMEOUT ) == RAL_IRQ_RTTOF_TIMEOUT )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id]                                          = RP_STATUS_RTTOF_TIMEOUT;\n            rp->radio_params[hook_id].rttof.ranging_result->distance_m   = 0;\n            rp->radio_params[hook_id].rttof.ranging_result->rssi         = 0;\n            rp->radio_params[hook_id].rttof.ranging_result->raw_distance = 0;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_TX_DONE ) == RAL_IRQ_TX_DONE )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_TX_DONE;\n            if( rp->priority_task.type == RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_LR_FHSS )\n            {\n                SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n                    ral_lr_fhss_handle_tx_done( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID,\n                                                &rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.lr_fhss.ral_lr_fhss_params,\n                                                NULL ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n\n                // fix issue with delay between the end of the transmission and the generation of txdone irq\n                // get delay according to lr-fhss params\n                uint16_t bit_delay_us = 0;\n                SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n                    ral_lr_fhss_get_bit_delay_in_us(\n                        TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, &rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.lr_fhss.ral_lr_fhss_params,\n                        rp->payload_buffer_size[hook_id], &bit_delay_us ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n                rp->irq_timestamp_ms[hook_id] = rp->irq_timestamp_ms[hook_id] - ( ( uint32_t ) bit_delay_us / 1000 );\n            }\n        }\n        else if( ( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RX_HDR_ERROR ) == RAL_IRQ_RX_HDR_ERROR ) ||\n                 ( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RX_CRC_ERROR ) == RAL_IRQ_RX_CRC_ERROR ) )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RX_CRC_ERROR;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RX_TIMEOUT ) == RAL_IRQ_RX_TIMEOUT )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RX_TIMEOUT;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_RX_DONE ) == RAL_IRQ_RX_DONE )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_RX_PACKET;\n\n            if( rp_get_pkt_payload( rp, &rp->tasks[hook_id] ) == RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR )\n            {\n                SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n                return;\n            }\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_CAD_OK ) == RAL_IRQ_CAD_OK )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_CAD_POSITIVE;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_CAD_DONE ) == RAL_IRQ_CAD_DONE )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_CAD_NEGATIVE;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_LR_FHSS_HOP ) == RAL_IRQ_LR_FHSS_HOP )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_LR_FHSS_HOP;\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n                ral_lr_fhss_handle_hop(\n                    TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, &rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.lr_fhss.ral_lr_fhss_params,\n                    ( ral_lr_fhss_memory_state_t ) rp->radio_params[hook_id].lr_fhss_state ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_WIFI_SCAN_DONE ) == RAL_IRQ_WIFI_SCAN_DONE )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_WIFI_SCAN_DONE;\n        }\n        else if( ( radio_irq & RAL_IRQ_GNSS_SCAN_DONE ) == RAL_IRQ_GNSS_SCAN_DONE )\n        {\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_GNSS_SCAN_DONE;\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: ERROR - IRQ source 0x%04X unknown\\n\", radio_irq );\n            rp->status[hook_id] = RP_STATUS_TASK_ABORTED;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nstatic void rp_task_compute_ranking( radio_planner_t* rp )\n{\n    uint8_t rank;\n    uint8_t ranks_temp[RP_NB_HOOKS];\n\n    for( int32_t i = 0; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n    {\n        ranks_temp[i] = rp->tasks[i].priority;\n    }\n    for( int32_t i = 0; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n    {\n        rank             = rp_task_find_highest_priority( &( ranks_temp[0] ), RP_NB_HOOKS );\n        ranks_temp[rank] = 0xFF;\n        rp->rankings[i]  = rank;\n    }\n}\n\nstatic void rp_task_launch_current( radio_planner_t* rp )\n{\n    uint8_t id = rp->radio_task_id;\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: Launch task #%u and start radio state %u, type %u\\n\", id, rp->tasks[id].state,\n                                    rp->tasks[id].type );\n    if( rp->tasks[id].launch_task_callbacks == NULL )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: ERROR - launch_task_callbacks == NULL \\n\" );\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        rp_task_print( rp, &rp->tasks[id] );\n        rp->radio = TARGET_RADIO;\n        rp->tasks[id].launch_task_callbacks( ( void* ) rp );\n    }\n}\n\nstatic uint8_t rp_task_select_next( radio_planner_t* rp, const uint32_t now )\n{\n    uint8_t  hook_to_exe_tmp      = 0xFF;\n    uint32_t hook_time_to_exe_tmp = 0;\n    uint32_t time_tmp             = 0;\n    uint8_t  rank                 = 0;\n    uint8_t  hook_id              = 0;\n\n    for( hook_id = 0; hook_id < RP_NB_HOOKS; hook_id++ )\n    {  // Garbage collector\n        if( ( rp->tasks[hook_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_SCHEDULE ) &&\n            ( ( ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[hook_id].start_time_ms - now ) < 0 ) ) )\n        {\n            rp->tasks[hook_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED;\n        }\n    }\n    for( hook_id = 0; hook_id < RP_NB_HOOKS; hook_id++ )\n    {\n        rank = rp->rankings[hook_id];\n        if( ( ( rp->tasks[rank].state < RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) &&\n              ( ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[rank].start_time_ms - now ) >= 0 ) ) ||\n            ( rp->tasks[rank].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) )\n        {\n            hook_to_exe_tmp      = rp->tasks[rank].hook_id;\n            hook_time_to_exe_tmp = rp->tasks[rank].start_time_ms;\n            break;\n        }\n    }\n    if( hook_id == RP_NB_HOOKS )\n    {\n        return RP_NO_MORE_TASK;\n    }\n\n    for( int32_t i = hook_id + 1; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n    {\n        rank = rp->rankings[i];\n        if( ( ( rp->tasks[rank].state < RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) &&\n              ( ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[rank].start_time_ms - now ) >= 0 ) ) ||\n            ( rp->tasks[rank].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) )\n        {\n            time_tmp = rp->tasks[rank].start_time_ms + rp->tasks[rank].duration_time_ms;\n\n            int32_t tmp = ( int32_t ) ( time_tmp - hook_time_to_exe_tmp );\n            if( ( tmp < 0 ) && ( ( int32_t ) ( time_tmp - now ) >= 0 ) )\n            {\n                hook_to_exe_tmp      = rp->tasks[rank].hook_id;\n                hook_time_to_exe_tmp = rp->tasks[rank].start_time_ms;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    rp->priority_task = rp->tasks[hook_to_exe_tmp];\n    return RP_SOMETHING_TO_DO;\n}\n\nstatic rp_next_state_status_t rp_task_get_next( radio_planner_t* rp, uint32_t* duration, uint8_t* task_id,\n                                                const uint32_t now )\n{\n    uint8_t  hook_id  = 0;\n    uint8_t  index    = 0xFF;\n    uint32_t time_tmp = now;\n\n    for( hook_id = 0; hook_id < RP_NB_HOOKS; hook_id++ )\n    {  // Garbage collector\n        if( ( rp->tasks[hook_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_SCHEDULE ) &&\n            ( ( ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[hook_id].start_time_ms - time_tmp ) < 0 ) ) )\n        {\n            rp->tasks[hook_id].state = RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED;\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"task schedule aborted because in the past %d\\n\",\n                                         ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[hook_id].start_time_ms - now ) );\n        }\n    }\n\n    // find the max time in the future\n    for( uint8_t i = 0; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n    {\n        if( ( ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[i].start_time_ms - time_tmp ) >= 0 ) )\n        {\n            time_tmp = rp->tasks[i].start_time_ms + ( RP_MARGIN_DELAY >> 1 );\n        }\n    }\n    for( uint8_t i = 0; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n\n    {  // set a timer only if a schedule task is pending and the radio activity is  running or for every task if the\n       // radio activity is not running\n\n        if(\n            // ( ( ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state == RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) &&\n            //     ( rp->tasks[i].state == RP_TASK_STATE_SCHEDULE ) ) ||\n            //   ( ( rp->tasks[rp->radio_task_id].state != RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) &&\n            ( rp->tasks[i].state < RP_TASK_STATE_RUNNING ) &&\n            ( ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[i].start_time_ms - time_tmp ) < 0 ) &&\n            ( ( int32_t ) ( rp->tasks[i].start_time_ms - now ) >= 0 ) )\n        {\n            time_tmp = rp->tasks[i].start_time_ms;\n            index    = i;\n        }\n    }\n    if( index == 0xFF )\n    {\n        return RP_STATUS_NO_MORE_TASK_SCHEDULE;\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        *task_id  = index;\n        *duration = time_tmp - now;\n        return RP_STATUS_HAVE_TO_SET_TIMER;\n    }\n}\nstatic uint8_t rp_task_find_highest_priority( uint8_t* vector, uint8_t length )\n{\n    uint8_t priority_high = 0xFF;\n    uint8_t index         = 0;\n\n    for( int32_t i = 0; i < length; i++ )\n    {\n        if( vector[i] <= priority_high )\n        {\n            priority_high = vector[i];\n            index         = i;\n        }\n    }\n    return index;\n}\n\nrp_hook_status_t rp_get_pkt_payload( radio_planner_t* rp, const rp_task_t* task )\n{\n    rp_hook_status_t status = RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n    uint8_t          id     = task->hook_id;\n\n    if( ( task->type == RP_TASK_TYPE_USER ) || ( task->type == RP_TASK_TYPE_NONE ) )\n    {\n        return status;  // don't catch the payload in case of user task\n    }\n\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE( ral_get_pkt_payload( &( rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[id]->ral ),\n                                                          rp->payload_buffer_size[id], rp->payload[id],\n                                                          &rp->rx_payload_size[id] ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n\n    if( ( task->type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_LORA ) || ( task->type == RP_TASK_TYPE_CAD_TO_RX ) )\n    {\n        rp->radio_params[id].pkt_type = RAL_PKT_TYPE_LORA;\n        status                        = RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n            ral_get_lora_rx_pkt_status( &( rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[id]->ral ),\n                                        &rp->radio_params[id].rx.lora_pkt_status ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n    }\n    else if( task->type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_FSK )\n    {\n        rp->radio_params[id].pkt_type = RAL_PKT_TYPE_GFSK;\n        status                        = RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n            ral_get_gfsk_rx_pkt_status( &( rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[id]->ral ),\n                                        &rp->radio_params[id].rx.gfsk_pkt_status ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n    }\n    else if( task->type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_FLRC )\n    {\n        rp->radio_params[id].pkt_type = RAL_PKT_TYPE_FLRC;\n        status                        = RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n            ral_get_flrc_rx_pkt_status( &( rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[id]->ral ),\n                                        &rp->radio_params[id].rx.flrc_pkt_status ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n    }\n    else if( ( task->type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE ) || ( task->type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE_SCAN ) )\n    {\n        rp->radio_params[id].pkt_type = RAL_PKT_TYPE_GFSK;\n        status                        = RP_HOOK_STATUS_OK;\n\n        // BLE using GFSK\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC_ON_FAILURE(\n            ral_get_gfsk_rx_pkt_status( &( rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[id]->ral ),\n                                        &rp->radio_params[id].rx.gfsk_pkt_status ) == RAL_STATUS_OK );\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        status = RP_HOOK_STATUS_ID_ERROR;\n    }\n\n    return status;\n}\n\nstatic void rp_set_alarm( radio_planner_t* rp, const uint32_t alarm_in_ms )\n{\n    smtc_modem_hal_stop_timer( );\n    smtc_modem_hal_start_timer( alarm_in_ms, rp_timer_irq_callback, rp );\n}\n\nstatic void rp_timer_irq( radio_planner_t* rp )\n{\n    rp_task_arbiter( rp, __func__ );\n}\n\nstatic void rp_task_call_aborted( radio_planner_t* rp )\n{\n    for( int32_t i = 0; i < RP_NB_HOOKS; i++ )\n    {\n        if( rp->tasks[i].state == RP_TASK_STATE_ABORTED )\n        {\n            SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" RP: INFO - Aborted hook # %d callback\\n\", i );\n            rp->stats.task_hook_aborted_nb[i]++;\n            rp_task_free( rp, &rp->tasks[i] );\n            rp->status[i] = RP_STATUS_TASK_ABORTED;\n            rp->radio     = rp->radio_target_attached_to_this_hook[i];\n            rp_hook_callback( rp, i );\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nstatic void rp_task_print( const radio_planner_t* rp, const rp_task_t* task )\n{\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \"\\n\" );\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP- INFO - Radio task #%u  running - Timer task #%u running  - Hook ID #%u -\",\n                                    rp->radio_task_id, rp->timer_hook_id, task->hook_id );\n    switch( task->type )\n    {\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_LORA:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_RX_LORA \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_FSK:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_RX_FSK \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_LORA:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_TX_LORA \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_FSK:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_TX_FSK \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_LR_FHSS:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_TX_LR_FHSS \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_CAD:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_CAD \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_CAD_TO_TX:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_CAD_TO_TX \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_CAD_TO_RX:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_CAD_TO_RX \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_BLE:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_TX_BLE \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_RX_BLE \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE_SCAN:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_RX_BLE_SCAN \" );\n        break;\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_NONE:\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_GNSS_SNIFF:\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_WIFI_SNIFF:\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_GNSS_RSSI:\n    case RP_TASK_TYPE_WIFI_RSSI:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_EMPTY \" );\n        break;\n    default:\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" TASK_ERROR \" );\n        break;\n    };\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_RP_TRACE_PRINTF( \" - start time @%u - priority #%u\\n\", task->start_time_ms, task->priority );\n}\n\nvoid print_hook_ids( void )\n{\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"Defined Hook IDs:\\n\" );\n\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_ID_SUSPEND: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_ID_SUSPEND );\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_RAC_VERY_HIGH_PRIORITY: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_RAC_VERY_HIGH_PRIORITY );\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_RAC_HIGH_PRIORITY: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_RAC_HIGH_PRIORITY );\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_RAC_MEDIUM_PRIORITY: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_RAC_MEDIUM_PRIORITY );\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_RAC_LOW_PRIORITY: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_RAC_LOW_PRIORITY );\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_RAC_VERY_LOW_PRIORITY: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_RAC_VERY_LOW_PRIORITY );\n\n#if defined( ADD_LBM_GEOLOCATION )\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_GNSS_ALMANAC: %d\\n\",\n                                 RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_GNSS_ALMANAC );\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_GNSS: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_ID_DIRECT_RP_ACCESS_GNSS RP_HOOK_ID_BLE_TX_BEACON );\n#endif\n\n#if defined( ADD_RELAY_RX )\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_ID_RELAY_RX_CAD: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_ID_RELAY_RX_CAD );\n#endif\n\n#if defined( ADD_RELAY_TX )\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_ID_RELAY_TX: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_ID_RELAY_TX );\n#if defined( ADD_CLASS_C )\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_ID_CLASS_C: %d\\n\", );\n#endif\n#else\n#if defined( ADD_CLASS_C )\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_ID_CLASS_C: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_ID_CLASS_C );\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_ID_MAX: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_ID_MAX );\n#else\n    SMTC_MODEM_HAL_TRACE_PRINTF( \"RP_HOOK_ID_MAX: %d\\n\", RP_HOOK_ID_MAX );\n#endif\n#endif\n}\nstatic void rp_consumption_statistics_updated( radio_planner_t* rp, const uint8_t hook_id, const uint32_t time )\n{\n    uint32_t micro_ampere_radio = 0, micro_ampere_process = 0;\n    uint32_t radio_t = 0, process_t = 0;\n    uint32_t tx_freq_hz = 0;\n\n    // TODO RP_TASK_TYPE_CAD_TO_TX, RP_TASK_TYPE_USER, RP_TASK_TYPE_NONE,\n\n    if( ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_LORA ) || ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_CAD ) ||\n        ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_CAD_TO_RX ) )\n    {\n        bool enable_boost_mode = false;\n        ral_cfg_rx_boosted( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, enable_boost_mode );\n        ral_get_lora_rx_consumption_in_ua( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, rp->radio_params[hook_id].rx.lora.mod_params.bw,\n                                           enable_boost_mode, &micro_ampere_radio );\n    }\n    else if( ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_FSK ) || ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_LBT ) )\n    {\n        bool enable_boost_mode = false;\n        ral_cfg_rx_boosted( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, enable_boost_mode );\n        ral_get_gfsk_rx_consumption_in_ua(\n            TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, rp->radio_params[hook_id].rx.gfsk.mod_params.br_in_bps,\n            rp->radio_params[hook_id].rx.gfsk.mod_params.bw_dsb_in_hz, enable_boost_mode, &micro_ampere_radio );\n    }\n    else if( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_LORA )\n    {\n        ral_get_tx_consumption_in_ua( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.lora.output_pwr_in_dbm,\n                                      rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.lora.rf_freq_in_hz, &micro_ampere_radio );\n        tx_freq_hz = rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.lora.rf_freq_in_hz;\n    }\n    else if( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_FSK )\n    {\n        ral_get_tx_consumption_in_ua( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.gfsk.output_pwr_in_dbm,\n                                      rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.gfsk.rf_freq_in_hz, &micro_ampere_radio );\n        tx_freq_hz = rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.gfsk.rf_freq_in_hz;\n    }\n    else if( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_FLRC )\n    {\n        ral_get_tx_consumption_in_ua( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.flrc.output_pwr_in_dbm,\n                                      rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.flrc.rf_freq_in_hz, &micro_ampere_radio );\n        tx_freq_hz = rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.flrc.rf_freq_in_hz;\n    }\n    else if( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_LR_FHSS )\n    {\n        // The power and duty-cycle are computed only on the center_frequency_in_hz and not on all hopping\n        ral_get_tx_consumption_in_ua( TARGET_RAL_FOR_HOOK_ID, rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.lr_fhss.output_pwr_in_dbm,\n                                      rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.lr_fhss.ral_lr_fhss_params.center_frequency_in_hz,\n                                      &micro_ampere_radio );\n\n        tx_freq_hz = rp->radio_params[hook_id].tx.lr_fhss.ral_lr_fhss_params.center_frequency_in_hz;\n    }\n\n    if( ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_GNSS_SNIFF ) ||\n        ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_GNSS_RSSI ) ||\n        ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_WIFI_SNIFF ) ||\n        ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_WIFI_RSSI ) )\n    {\n        rp_stats_sniff_update( &rp->stats, time, radio_t, process_t, hook_id, micro_ampere_radio,\n                               micro_ampere_process );\n    }\n    else if( ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_TX_BLE ) || ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE ) ||\n             ( rp->tasks[hook_id].type == RP_TASK_TYPE_RX_BLE_SCAN ) )\n    {\n        // TODO for this kind of task\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        uint32_t tx_timestamp_tmp = rp->stats.tx_timestamp;\n        rp_stats_update( &rp->stats, time, hook_id, micro_ampere_radio );\n        if( tx_timestamp_tmp != 0 )\n        {\n            smtc_duty_cycle_sum( tx_freq_hz, rp->stats.tx_last_toa_ms[hook_id] );\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- CALLBACK FUNCTIONS DEFINITION -------------------------------------------\n */\n\nvoid rp_radio_irq_callback( void* obj )\n{\n    radio_planner_t* rp                     = ( ( radio_planner_t* ) obj );\n    rp->radio_irq_flag                      = true;\n    rp->irq_timestamp_ms[rp->radio_task_id] = smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( );\n    smtc_modem_hal_user_lbm_irq( );\n}\n\nstatic void rp_timer_irq_callback( void* obj )\n{\n    radio_planner_t* rp = ( ( radio_planner_t* ) obj );\n    rp->timer_irq_flag  = true;\n    smtc_modem_hal_user_lbm_irq( );\n}\n\nstatic void rp_hook_callback( radio_planner_t* rp, uint8_t id )\n{\n    if( id >= RP_NB_HOOKS )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return;\n    }\n    if( rp->hook_callbacks[id] == NULL )\n    {\n        SMTC_MODEM_HAL_PANIC( );\n        return;\n    }\n    rp->radio_is_free = false;  // this is a kind of critical section\n    rp->hook_callbacks[id]( rp->hooks[id] );\n    rp->radio_is_free = true;\n}\n\n/* --- EOF ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n"
```json
  }
}
```

---

## MODEL ✨

**Analyzing Radio Planner** I've been digging into the Radio Planner and RAC, specifically identifying a busy-wait loop in `smtc_rac_lora.c` that needs addressing.**Investigating Callback Blocks** I'm examining the `launch_task_callbacks` within the Radio Planner. It appears the `usp_main_thread` is blocking when `rp_callback` triggers a future task launch, leading to a busy-wait for LoRa Studio's synchronization.**Identifying Sleep Issue** My current focus is on the `thread.c` implementation. I've found that when `CONFIG_USP_LORA_BASICS_MODEM` is not defined, the main thread sleeps for a lengthy 60 seconds, and I'm now investigating if `smtc_rac_submit_radio_transaction` can actually trigger an interrupt to break this extended sleep.**Tracing Transaction Submission** I've traced `smtc_rac_submit_radio_transaction`'s execution path. If called from the main thread, the callback's busy-wait loop will indeed halt that thread, confirming my previous suspicion about the main thread blocking.**Tracing Callback Execution** I've confirmed that the `smtc_rac_rx_callback` initiates a busy-wait loop immediately after the `pre_ping_pong_callback` is executed. This callback is directly invoked within `smtc_rac_rx_callback`, so the delay is happening exactly where suspected.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "read_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "application/samples/usp/sdk/ping_pong/src/main.c"
  },
  "id": "read_file_1779290019590_0"
}
```

This is set by the libraray during \"critical\"\n * sections\n */\nstatic bool prv_modem_irq_enabled = true;\nstatic bool prv_modem_irq_pending_while_disabled;\nstatic bool prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer, prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer_handler, NULL );\n\n/* context and callback for the event pin interrupt */\nstatic void* prv_smtc_modem_hal_radio_irq_context;\nstatic void ( *prv_smtc_modem_hal_radio_irq_callback )( void* context );\n\n/* ------------ Initialization ------------\n *\n * This function is defined in lorawan_hal_init.h\n * and is used to set everything up in prv_transceiver_dev );\n#endif\n}\n\n/* ------------ System management ------------ */\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_reset_mcu( void )\n{\n    LOG_WRN( \"Resetting the MCU\" );\n#if defined( CONFIG_LOG )\n    log_panic( ); /* To flush the logs */\n#endif\n    k_msleep( 100 );\n    sys_reboot( SYS_REBOOT_COLD );\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_reload_wdog( void )\n{\n    /* This is only provided for internal debugging purposes, so it was\n     * decided not to implement it in the Zephyr port.\n     */\n}\n\nuint32_t smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_s( void )\n{\n    return k_uptime_seconds( );\n}\n\nuint32_t smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms( void )\n{\n    /* The wrapping every 49 days is expected by the modem lib */\n    return k_uptime_get_32( );\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_set_offset_to_test_wrapping( const uint32_t offset_to_test_wrapping )\n{\n    /* This aims to add a virtual offset to values returned by smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms.\n     * This is only provided for internal development purposes, so it was\n     * decided not to implement it in the Zephyr port.\n     */\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_interruptible_msleep( k_timeout_t timeout )\n{\n    /* Sleep until we are notified by smtc_modem_hal_wake_up(). */\n    k_sem_take( &lbm_main_loop_sem, timeout );\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_wake_up( void )\n{\n    /* Notify the main loop if it's sleeping */\n    k_sem_give( &lbm_main_loop_sem );\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_user_lbm_irq( void )\n{\n    smtc_modem_hal_wake_up( );\n}\n\nstruct k_sem* smtc_modem_hal_get_event_sem( void )\n{\n    return &lbm_main_loop_sem;\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_protect_api_call( void )\n{\n    // Do nothing in case implementation is bare metal\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_unprotect_api_call( void )\n{\n    // Do nothing in case implementation is bare metal\n}\n\n/* ------------ Timer management ------------ */\n\n/**\n * @brief Called when the prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer expires.\n *\n * Submits the prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer_work to be handle the callback.\n */\nstatic void prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer_handler( struct k_timer* timer )\n{\n    ARG_UNUSED( timer );\n\n    if( prv_modem_irq_enabled )\n    {\n        prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer_callback( prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer_context );\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        prv_modem_irq_pending_while_disabled = true;\n    }\n};\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_start_timer( const uint32_t milliseconds, void ( *callback )( void* context ), void* context )\n{\n    prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer_callback = callback;\n    prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer_context  = context;\n\n    /* start one-shot timer */\n    k_timer_start( &prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer, K_MSEC( milliseconds ), K_NO_WAIT );\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_stop_timer( void )\n{\n    k_timer_stop( &prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer );\n}\n\n/* ------------ IRQ management ------------ */\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_disable_modem_irq( void )\n{\n    prv_modem_irq_enabled = false;\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_enable_modem_irq( void )\n{\n    prv_modem_irq_enabled = true;\n    lora_transceiver_board_enable_interrupt( prv_transceiver_dev );\n\n    if( prv_radio_irq_pending_while_disabled )\n    {\n        prv_radio_irq_pending_while_disabled = false;\n        prv_smtc_modem_hal_radio_irq_callback( prv_smtc_modem_hal_radio_irq_context );\n    }\n    if( prv_modem_irq_pending_while_disabled )\n    {\n        prv_modem_irq_pending_while_disabled = false;\n        prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer_callback( prv_smtc_modem_hal_timer_context );\n    }\n}\n\n/* ------------ Panic management ------------ */\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_on_panic( uint8_t* func, uint32_t line, const char* fmt, ... )\n{\n    const size_t buffer_size = 255;\n    uint8_t      buffer[buffer_size];\n    uint8_t      length;\n    va_list      args;\n\n    /* NOTE: uint8_t *func parameter is actually __func__ casted to uint8_t*,\n     * so it can be safely printed with %s\n     */\n    length = snprintf( ( char* ) buffer, buffer_size, \"%s:%u \", func, line );\n    va_start( args, fmt );\n    length += vsnprintf( ( char* ) buffer + length, buffer_size - length, fmt, args );\n    va_end( args );\n\n    LOG_ERR( \"Modem panic: %s\", buffer );\n\n    /* NOTE: smtc_modem_hal_crashlog_set_status(true) is done by\n     * smtc_modem_hal_crashlog_store() for simplicity of flash usage\n     */\n    smtc_modem_hal_crashlog_store( buffer, length );\n\n    smtc_modem_hal_reset_mcu( );\n}\n\n/* ------------ Random management ------------ */\n\nuint32_t smtc_modem_hal_get_random_nb_in_range( const uint32_t val_1, const uint32_t val_2 )\n{\n    /* Implementation copied from the lbm_examples */\n    uint32_t min   = MIN( val_1, val_2 );\n    uint32_t max   = MAX( val_1, val_2 );\n    uint32_t range = ( max - min + 1 );\n\n    /* Fix cases when val1=0, val2=UINT32_MAX */\n    range = range ? range : UINT32_MAX;\n    return ( uint32_t ) ( ( sys_rand32_get( ) % range ) + min );\n}\n\n/* ------------ Radio env management ------------ */\n\n/**\n * @brief Called when the transceiver event pin interrupt is triggered.\n *\n * If CONFIG_LORA_BASICS_MODEM_DRIVERS_EVENT_TRIGGER_GLOBAL_THREAD=y,\n * this is called in the system workq.\n * If CONFIG_LORA_BASICS_MODEM_DRIVERS_EVENT_TRIGGER_OWN_THREAD=y,\n * this is called in the transceiver event thread.\n *\n * @param[in] dev The transceiver device.\n */\nvoid prv_transceiver_event_cb( const struct device* dev )\n{\n    if( prv_modem_irq_enabled )\n    {\n        /* Due to the way the transceiver driver is implemented,\n         * this is called from the system workq.\n         */\n        prv_smtc_modem_hal_radio_irq_callback( prv_smtc_modem_hal_radio_irq_context );\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        prv_radio_irq_pending_while_disabled = true;\n    }\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_irq_config_radio_irq( void ( *callback )( void* context ), void* context )\n{\n    /* save callback function and context */\n    prv_smtc_modem_hal_radio_irq_context  = context;\n    prv_smtc_modem_hal_radio_irq_callback = callback;\n\n    /* enable callback via transceiver driver */\n    lora_transceiver_board_attach_interrupt( prv_transceiver_dev, prv_transceiver_event_cb );\n    lora_transceiver_board_enable_interrupt( prv_transceiver_dev );\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_radio_irq_clear_pending( void )\n{\n    prv_radio_irq_pending_while_disabled = false;\n}\n\nbool smtc_modem_external_stack_currently_use_radio( void )\n{\n    /* return false if the radio is available for the lbm stack\n     * This is not supported yet.\n     */\n    return false;\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_start_radio_tcxo( void )\n{\n    /* We only support TCXO's that are wired to the transceiver.\n     * In such cases, this function must be empty according to the porting guide.\n     */\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_stop_radio_tcxo( void )\n{\n    /* We only support TCXO's that are wired to the transceiver.\n     * In such cases, this function must be empty according to the porting guide.\n     */\n}\n\nuint32_t smtc_modem_hal_get_radio_tcxo_startup_delay_ms( void )\n{\n    /* From the porting guide:\n     * If the TCXO is configured by the RAL BSP to start up automatically, then the value used\n     * here should be the same as the startup delay used in the RAL BSP.\n     * https://github.com/Lora-net/SWL2001/blob/master/lbm_lib/PORTING_GUIDE.md#uint32_t-smtc_modem_hal_get_radio_tcxo_startup_delay_ms-void-\n     */\n    return lora_transceiver_get_tcxo_startup_delay_ms( prv_transceiver_dev );\n}\n\nvoid smtc_modem_hal_set_ant_switch( bool is_tx_on )\n{\n    /* NOTE: We only support antenna switches managed by the transceiver.\n     */\n}\n\n/* ------------ Environment management ------------ */\n\nvoid lorawan_register_battery_level_callback( lorawan_battery_level_cb_t cb )\n{\n    battery_level_cb = cb;\n}\n\nvoid lorawan_register_battery_voltage_callback( lorawan_battery_voltage_cb_t cb )\n{\n    battery_voltage_cb = cb;\n}\n\nvoid lorawan_register_temperature_callback( lorawan_temperature_cb_t cb )\n{\n    temperature_cb = cb;\n}\n\nuint8_t smtc_modem_hal_get_battery_level( void )\n{\n    if( battery_level_cb )\n    {\n        return battery_level_cb( );\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        return 255;\n    }\n}\n\nuint16_t smtc_modem_hal_get_voltage_mv( void )\n{\n    if( battery_voltage_cb )\n    {\n        return battery_voltage_cb( );\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        return 0;\n   }

---

## MODEL ✨

**Analyzing Busy-Wait Blocks** I'm currently pinpointing the root cause of the busy-wait loop's blockage. It appears `smtc_modem_hal_get_time_in_ms` is standard Zephyr and not the culprit. My focus is now on how `rp->tasks[id].start_time_ms` might be disproportionately large.**Investigating Future Timestamps** I've identified a critical loop in `smtc_rac_lora.c` where `rp->tasks[id].start_time_ms` is compared against the current time. If this `start_time_ms` is set far into the future, it creates a prolonged busy-wait. My next step is to trace why this value is being set in the future within `app_ping_pong.c`.**Tracing Future Timestamps** I'm now digging into the Radio Planner's logic. It seems a scheduled task *must* be in the future. If Ping Pong's initial `ASAP` request is processed correctly by `rp_task_enqueue`, setting the start time to 'now', then the issue likely lies elsewhere, perhaps in how this time is later interpreted or updated.**Examining Time Initialization** I'm re-examining `rp_task_enqueue` and how ASAP tasks are handled. It appears `start_time_ms` isn't explicitly updated for ASAP tasks during enqueueing. My current focus is tracking where this value *is* updated, specifically within `rp_task_update_time`, where it seems to be set to `now + fairness_tmp`, which should be a minimal delay.**Tool Command**:

---

## MODEL ✨

**Updating Initialization Logic** I'm currently reviewing the initialization flow, specifically how `SMTC_SW_PLATFORM_INIT()` interacts with `zephyr_usp_initialization_wait()` to ensure the `usp_main_thread` is ready. My focus is on the conditional use of mutexes based on `CONFIG_USP_THREADS_MUTEXES`, aiming to refine the process for optimal thread synchronization.**Analyzing Race Condition** The `CONFIG_USP_THREADS_MUTEXES` setting being commented out indicates no mutex protection between the main and USP threads. This creates a race condition when `ping_pong_on_button_press` calls radio functions concurrently with `smtc_rac_run_engine`. This appears to be the root cause of the observed hangs, as opposed to the display driver issue.**Investigating Blocking Calls** I'm now exploring potential blocking calls within the RAC module. The log indicating the FSM is calling RAC and the module creating a logical barrier to wait for a packet from LoRa Studio has me re-examining `smtc_rac_lora.c`. I suspect `rp_task_enqueue` might be the culprit, potentially blocking the thread.**Investigating Busy-Wait** I've identified a critical busy-wait loop within `radio_planner.c`. This loop could potentially hang indefinitely if `task->start_time_ms` is excessively large. I suspect this is related to the "LoRa Studio" mode, which likely involves a `RP_TASK_TYPE_LOCK_RADIO_ACCESS` task, and its interaction with `smtc_rac_lock_radio_access`.**Tool Command**:

## MODEL ✨

**Analyzing Configuration Options** I'm currently examining the implications of `CONFIG_USP_THREADS_MUTEXES`. It appears that if this is disabled, the `SMTC_SW_PLATFORM` macro effectively becomes inert, which is a crucial observation for understanding our thread synchronization behavior.**Investigating Race Condition** I'm focusing on a potential race condition where both the main and USP threads might be concurrently accessing the Radio Planner. The log indicating a transaction start but subsequent blocking in a `while` loop at `smtc_rac_lora.c` strongly suggests this.**Tool Command**:

## MODEL ✨

**Analyzing Fairness Delay** I'm currently investigating the `RP_MCU_FAIRNESS_DELAY_MS` parameter, which appears to be linked to `RP_MARGIN_DELAY`. I'm trying to pinpoint where `RP_MARGIN_DELAY` is defined, as it typically sits around 2 or 4. The user mentioned LoRa Studio, prompting me to consider if `RP_TASK_ASAP_TO_SCHEDULE_TRIG_TIME` has been met.**Investigating Latency Contributors** I've identified that the "asap" task switches to scheduled after 120 seconds. The `ping_pong_rx(ASAP, NO_DELAY)` call at init within `app_ping_pong.c` seems crucial, especially if `usp_main_thread` is delayed or `rp_callback` is infrequent, leading to queue buildup. The "hardware modem" feel likely stems from `CONFIG_USP_MAIN_THREAD=y` with `CONFIG_USP_THREADS_MUTEXES` off, potentially causing race conditions. The busy-wait loop in `smtc_rac_lora.c` is also a strong suspect for blocking.**Analyzing Processing Delay** I've discovered a potential bottleneck related to `SUBORDINATE_PROCESSING_TIME_MS`, which is 10ms by default. It seems when I receive a PING, I schedule a PONG for `now + 10ms`. However, the Radio Planner's actual launch time is adjusted by `margin_delay`, which is concerning. I'm also looking into how interrupts affect this.**Investigating Configuration Overrides** I've identified that the `SUBORDINATE_PROCESSING_TIME_MS` could be overridden to a very large value, like 5000ms, potentially causing significant blocking. I'm currently examining build configurations, specifically `CMakeLists.txt` and `prj.conf` files, to determine if and why such an override might be occurring.**Tool Command**:

```json
    "output": "/**\n * @file      smtc_rac_api.h\n *\n * @brief     Header file for smtc_rac API\n *\n * This file provides the API for the RAC, which manages radio access,\n * scheduling, and configuration for LoRa and ranging operations. It defines the\n * main data structures, enums, and function prototypes for interacting with the\n * radio planner and hardware abstraction.\n *\n * The API allows applications to:\n *   - Initialize and run the RAC engine.\n *   - Request radio access with a given priority and callback.\n *   - Configure LoRa and ranging parameters for transmission and reception.\n *   - Schedule radio tasks with precise timing.\n *   - Access radio event data such as RSSI, SNR, and timestamps.\n *   - Enqueue LoRa or ranging tasks for execution by the radio planner.\n *\n * The API is designed to be hardware-agnostic and supports multiple radio\n * chipsets.\n *\n * The main structures are:\n *   - smtc_rac_radio_lora_params_t: Holds all radio parameters for LoRa and\n * ranging operations.\n *   - smtc_rac_data_t: Holds payload, result, and event data for a radio\n * transaction.\n *   - smtc_rac_scheduler_config_t: Holds scheduling and callback information\n * for a radio task.\n *   - smtc_rac_context_t: Groups all the above for a complete radio\n * transaction context.\n *\n * The API also defines enums for radio access priority and return codes.\n *\n * The RAC is intended to be used in embedded applications requiring\n * precise and efficient management of radio resources, such as LoRaWAN,\n * ranging, and frequency hopping protocols.\n *\n * The Clear BSD License\n * Copyright Semtech Corporation 2025.       /*!< Data result from the transaction. */\n\n    // optional parameters\n    smtc_rac_lbt_context_t      lbt_context; /*!< LBT context for Listen Before Talk operations. */\n    smtc_rac_cad_radio_params_t cad_context; /*!< CAD context for Channel Activity Detection operations. */\n    smtc_rac_cw_context_t       cw_context;  /*!< CW context for Continuous Wave operations. */\n\n} smtc_rac_context_t;\n\n/**\n * @brief USP RAC API version structure definition\n */\ntypedef struct smtc_usp_rac_version_s\n{\n    uint8_t major;  //!< Major value\n    uint8_t minor;  //!< Minor value\n    uint8_t patch;  //!< Patch value\n} smtc_usp_rac_version_t;\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PUBLIC API - CORE FUNCTIONS --------------------------------------------\n */\n\n/**\n * @brief Get the USP RAC API version\n *\n * @param [out] USP RAC API version\n *\n * @return return code as defined in @ref smtc_rac_return_code_t\n * @retval SMTC_RAC_SUCCESS                Command executed without errors\n * @retval SMTC_RAC_INVALID_PARAMETER       \\p version is NULL\n */\nsmtc_rac_return_code_t smtc_rac_get_version( smtc_usp_rac_version_t* version );\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Initializes the RAC.\n *\n * This function must be called before any other RAC API function.\n * It initializes the radio hardware, puts it in sleep mode, and sets up the\n * radio planner.\n */\nvoid smtc_rac_init( void );\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Runs the RAC engine.\n *\n * This function should be called regularly (e.g., in the main loop) to process\n * radio events and tasks.\n */\nvoid smtc_rac_run_engine( void );\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Checks if an IRQ flag is pending.\n *\n * \\return True if an IRQ flag is pending, false otherwise.\n */\nbool smtc_rac_is_irq_flag_pending( void );\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PUBLIC API - RADIO ACCESS MANAGEMENT -----------------------------------\n */\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Requests radio access.\n *\n * Registers a callback to be called when the radio is available at the given\n * priority.\n *\n * \\param [in] priority Priority of the request.\n *\n * \\return Radio access ID (used for future transactions),\n * RAC_INVALID_RADIO_ID if the request fails.\n */\nuint8_t smtc_rac_open_radio( smtc_rac_priority_t priority );\n\n/*\n * \\brief Closes the radio access.\n *\n * This function releases the radio access associated with the given radio\n * access ID. It should be called when the radio is no longer needed.\n *\n * \\param [in] radio_access_id The radio access ID obtained from\n * smtc_rac_open_radio.\n *\n * \\return Return code indicating success or error.\n */\nsmtc_rac_return_code_t smtc_rac_close_radio( uint8_t radio_access_id );\n\n/*\n * \\brief Submit a radio transaction.\n *\n * This function submits a radio transaction for execution by the radio planner.\n *\n * \\param [in] radio_access_id The radio access ID obtained from\n * smtc_rac_open_radio.\n */\nsmtc_rac_return_code_t smtc_rac_submit_radio_transaction( uint8_t radio_access_id );\n\n/*\n * \\brief Aborts a radio submit.\n *\n * This function aborts a pending radio request associated with the given radio\n * access ID. It can be used to cancel a scheduled or in-progress radio\n * transaction.\n *\n * \\param [in] radio_access_id The radio access ID obtained from\n * smtc_rac_open_radio.\n *\n * \\return Return code indicating success or error.\n */\nsmtc_rac_return_code_t smtc_rac_abort_radio_submit( uint8_t radio_access_id );\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PUBLIC API - CONTEXT AND DRIVER ACCESS ---------------------------------\n */\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Gets the radio planner instance.\n *\n * \\return Pointer to the radio planner instance.\n */\nradio_planner_t* smtc_rac_get_rp( void );\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Gets the ralf_t instance.\n *\n * \\return Pointer to the ralf_t instance.\n */\nralf_t* smtc_rac_get_radio( void );\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Gets the RAC context for a specific radio access ID.\n *\n * This functions returns the complete context of the radio transaction\n * associated to the radio access ID. All fields are initialized to 0.\n * The caller is responsible for setting:\n * - modulation_type and the associated radio_params\n * - smtc_rac_data_buffer_setup\n * - scheduler_config (except duration_time_ms)\n * - (optionally) lbt_context, cad_context, cw_context\n * before calling smtc_rac_submit_radio_transaction(radio_access_id).\n * The results of the transaction will be available for reading in:\n * - smtc_rac_data_buffer_setup\n * - smtc_rac_data_result\n * - scheduler_config.duration_time_ms\n * when scheduler_config.callback_post_radio_transaction() is invoked.\n *\n * \\param [in] radio_access_id The radio access ID obtained from\n * smtc_rac_open_radio.\n *\n * \\return Pointer to the RAC context for the specified radio access ID.\n */\nsmtc_rac_context_t* smtc_rac_get_context( uint8_t radio_access_id );\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PUBLIC API - SPECIALIZED OPERATIONS ------------------------------------\n */\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Direct radio driver access.\n *\n * This function allows direct access to the radio driver.\n * \\note The radio access is locked if your request is granted, when thge radio is lock first rac will call the\n * callback_pre_radio_transaction . In this function you can prepare the radio for the transaction.\n * When the transaction is finished, rac will call the callback_post_radio_transaction with the status\n * RP_STATUS_RADIO_LOCKED if the transaction is successful, RP_STATUS_TASK_ABORTED if the transaction\n * is aborted. At this stage the radio is still locked and you can continue to use the radio. If you want to unlock the\n radio,\n * you can call smtc_rac_unlock_radio_access.\n\n * \\param [in] radio_access_id The radio access ID obtained from\n * smtc_rac_open_radio.\n * \\param [in] scheduler_config The scheduler configuration.\n *\n * \\return Return code indicating success or error.\n */\nsmtc_rac_return_code_t smtc_rac_lock_radio_access( uint8_t                     radio_access_id,\n                                                   smtc_rac_scheduler_config_t scheduler_config );\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Unlocks the radio access.\n *\n * This function unlocks the radio access associated with the given radio\n * access ID. This function should be called when the radio access get with smtc_rac_lock_radio_access is no longer\n *needed.\n * \\note  if you unlock the radio access without locking it first, the behavior is the same as if you have locked it\n *first and then unlocked it. as a consequence the callback_post_radio_transaction will called with the status\n *RP_STATUS_TASK_UNLOCKED.\n * \\param [in] radio_access_id The radio access ID obtained from\n * smtc_rac_open_radio.\n *\\return Return code indicating success or error.\n */\nsmtc_rac_return_code_t smtc_rac_unlock_radio_access( uint8_t radio_access_id );\n/*!\n * \\brief Gets the radio driver context instance.\n *\n * \\return Pointer to the radio driver context instance.\n */\nvoid* smtc_rac_get_radio_driver_context( void );\n\n/*\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * --- PUBLIC API - SET RADIO CONTEXT -----------------------------------------\n */\n\n/*!\n * \\brief Set the Radio Context (will be used in radio implementation, for\n * examples gpio management or a reset). \\note To be called before\n * smtc_rac_init()\n *\n * \\param [in] radio_ctx pointer to transceiver implemented by OS/baremetal.\n */\nvoid smtc_rac_set_radio_context( const void* radio_ctx );\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\n}\n#endif\n\n#endif  // RAC_H\n"
  }
}
```

---

## MODEL ✨

**Discovering Anomalies** I've been reviewing the API, and initially, nothing stood out as unusual. However, a recent inspection of the user's `prj.conf` file for Ping Pong has revealed some interesting configurations related to LoRa drivers. I'm now investigating the implications of these settings within `main.c`.**Investigating LoRa Drivers** My focus has shifted to the LBM drivers included in the Ping Pong sample. Although the Modem itself isn't explicitly configured, these drivers appear to be active and are processing radio interrupts through a callback mechanism, which warrants deeper inspection.**Analyzing RX Callback** I've traced the radio interrupts. User LBM IRQ triggers a wakeup semaphore for the USP thread. Intriguingly, the initial RX setup involves a busy-wait loop within the `main` thread, which is concerning if the receive start time is delayed, potentially causing a hang.**Confirming RAC Behavior** I've identified a crucial detail related to the device tree configuration. It seems the RAC's master control over the radio was not properly established, leading it to erroneously wait for external input from LoRa Studio. I'm now re-examining `smtc_rac_submit_radio_transaction`.**Investigating RP Failsafe** I've noticed a failsafe mechanism within the radio planner that triggers a panic if a task exceeds 128 seconds. This is a critical point to investigate in relation to previous observations about potential hangs during receive setup.**Confirming Task Initiation** I've confirmed that the `usp/rac: transaction is starting` log indeed signals the RAC's acceptance and imminent launch of the task. The hang is occurring within the busy-wait loop in `smtc_rac_lora.c`, likely due to the Radio Planner not running as expected or a race condition between threads.**Detecting Race Conditions** I've identified a critical race condition. With mutexes disabled, simultaneous modifications to the `radio_planner` structure by the `usp_main_thread` and `main` thread, particularly during `rp_callback` and `smtc_rac_submit_radio_transaction` calls, are causing instability.**Enabling Mutexes** I've pinpointed a critical race condition related to simultaneous modifications of the `radio_planner` structure. Given your report of a stall within a `while` loop in `smtc_rac_lora.c` after the `usp/rac: transaction is starting` log, I strongly suspect this is the root cause. My current thought is to suggest enabling mutexes to mitigate this instability. I'll also consider the potential impact of `SUBORDINATE_PROCESSING_TIME_MS`, though direct verification isn't possible from my end.**Tool Command**:
